               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Sunday
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oriikAMmXXw/UxKbYeGgimI/AAAAAAAAUTI/PkJn9b0Je2Q/s1600/introvert6.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="9061871738959415695" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="5277645522786077953" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="5277645522786077953">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Are You An Introvert Like Me, And How To Best Live Your Life.
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5277645522786077953" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.jamesdazouloute.net/2014/03/are-you-introvert-like-me-and-how-to.html" target="_blank">
                        <img alt=" Are you an introvert like me.." border="0" height="196" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-oriikAMmXXw/UxKbYeGgimI/AAAAAAAAUTI/PkJn9b0Je2Q/s1600/introvert6.jpg" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <span style="color: #4c4c4c;">
                          <br/>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <span style="color: #4c4c4c;">
                          "Introverts  people with quieter and more reflective personalities  who typically thrive within the inner workings of their own minds, and love to be alone". And those kind of people do not fit in well with Society or their Peers. So of course as you can imagine, Society will never give you a moment's peace until you fall in line with what they expect you to be, which is just like them. And if you don't, then they will label you, they will diagnose you, they will seek to treat you to become like them, and if that doesn't work then they will begin to persecute you. All the while proclaiming through their hypocrisy that the world is a richly diverse place and everyone is special and different.
                         </span>
                         <u>
                          <span style="color: red;">
                           Case And Point:
                          </span>
                         </u>
                         <span style="color: #4c4c4c;">
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #4c4c4c; font-size: 14px; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         in
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         2010, the American Psychiatric Association even considered classifying
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://www.psychologytoday.com/blog/self-promotion-introverts/201008/giant-step-backward-introverts" sl-processed="1" style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #6aa3b1; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; orphans: 2; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none; widows: 2;" target="_hplink">
                         "introverted personality"
                        </a>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         as a disorder by listing it in the Diagnostic and Statistical Manual (DSM-5), a manual used to diagnose mental illness.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.jamesdazouloute.net/2014/03/are-you-introvert-like-me-and-how-to.html" target="_blank">
                        <img alt=" The life of introverts..." border="0" height="481" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-nbOuf2D6i7k/UxKbpQNqquI/AAAAAAAAUTQ/3SnXP1P0iRY/s1600/introver1.jpg" width="640"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <span style="font-size: 15px;">
                          So do you see my friend? For us Introverts who like to spend time alone and live in our own heads, but love to interact with others occasionally, the world can easily misunderstand us. And then they will say that you are weird, that you are not like the easily lovable Extroverts, who just can't keep their mouth shut, who love to be the life of the party, who have to start conversations just for the sake of talking, who get a big rush of Dopamine just being part of a crowd, and who don't mind being hypocrites with all people whom they deal with.
                         </span>
                         <u>
                          <span style="font-size: large;">
                           But as for you Introvert,
                          </span>
                         </u>
                         <span style="font-size: 15px;">
                          you love to think, you love to put things together in your mind, you love to study people and watch their behavior, you love to write and teach others, you love to spend time alone and enjoy all kind of things. But sometime you don't mind talking with others, you don't mind helping others, you don't mind giving of yourself and you certainly want to make the world a better place by having all people to be fair, just, truthful and loving toward one another.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.jamesdazouloute.net/2014/03/are-you-introvert-like-me-and-how-to.html" target="_blank">
                        <img alt=" How to piss off an introvert..." border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YzFO3Ox5ksY/UxKb6nnd6nI/AAAAAAAAUTc/3Uz9mvh73VY/s1600/introvert2.png"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         So why can't the world leave you alone, why can't your friends and family just be there for you just in case? Instead of always accusing you of something being wrong with you? And why must they always force you to talk constantly, why drag you out of your home, why force you be around them 24 hours a day? And just because they are very dependent on others and must be going out and do something every second of the day, they seem to think that you, as an Introvert, have the same needs and wants as they do. But funny thing is, you don't judge them as Extroverts, you don't label them, you don't force your will on them and you certainly don't persecute them. And so this is why today I have written this article for you, just so you can understand yourself better, and just so you can share this information with them, and that way you and them can finally live in harmony and respect each other's different wants and needs in this life. James Dazouloute, An Introvert Like You.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>

                       <br/>
                      </span>

                        As an Introvert, this looks like the only place you ever want to be forever and ever.

                       <h2 style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-family: ProximaNovaSemibold, Helvetica, Arial; font-size: 26px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        Because being an introvert means youre a really great listener.
                       </h2>
                       <div class="sub_buzz_content" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; line-height: 0; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 3px; position: relative;">
                        <div class="share-box" style="background-color: #fafafa; border-bottom-left-radius: 4px; border-bottom-right-radius: 4px; border-top-left-radius: 4px; border-top-right-radius: 4px; border: 1px solid rgb(231, 231, 231); left: -15px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 5px 0px; position: absolute; top: 5px; visibility: hidden; width: 38px; z-index: 999; zoom: 1;">
                         <a class="share-icon bf_dom sub-buzz-facebook-share" href="https://www.blogger.com/null" id="facebook2281761_1229952" rel:bf_bucket_data="{'fb-share':{'id':'2281761_1229952'}}" rel:gt_act="share/facebook/list-item:28" rel:gt_label="/static/enhanced/webdr02/2013/5/31/16/enhanced-buzz-31095-1370032283-12.jpg" rel:sub_title="Because being an introvert means you're a really great listener." style="background-image: url(http://s3-ak.buzzfed.com/static/images/public/icons/large-share-sprite24x24.png?v=201402281627); background-position: 0px -24px; background-repeat: no-repeat no-repeat; border: 0px; color: #0077ee; float: left; height: 24px !important; margin: 3px 7px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; width: 24px !important;">
                         </a>

                      <u>
                       <span style="color: red;">
                        <br class="Apple-interchange-newline"/>
                       </span>
                      </u>
                      <br/>
                      <h1 style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 30px; font-weight: 500; letter-spacing: 1px; line-height: 25px; orphans: 2; padding: 0px; text-align: center; text-shadow: rgb(225, 218, 212) 0px 0px 1px; widows: 2;">
                       <u>
                        <span style="color: red;">
                         10 Myths/Facts About Introverts
                        </span>
                       </u>
                      </h1>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #1  Introverts dont like to talk
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       This is not true. Introverts just dont talk unless they have something to say. They hate small talk. Get an introvert talking about something they are interested in, and they wont shut up for days.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #2  Introverts are shy.
                       </strong>
                       <br/>
                       Shyness has nothing to do with being an Introvert. Introverts are not necessarily afraid of people. What they need is a reason to interact. They dont interact for the sake of interacting. If you want to talk to an Introvert, just start talking. Dont worry about being polite.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #3  Introverts are rude
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Introverts often dont see a reason for beating around the bush with social pleasantries. They want everyone to just be real and honest. Unfortunately, this is not acceptable in most settings, so Introverts can feel a lot of pressure to fit in, which they find exhausting.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #4  Introverts dont like people
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       On the contrary, Introverts intensely value the few friends they have. They can count their close friends on one hand. If you are lucky enough for an introvert to consider you a friend, you probably have a loyal ally for life. Once you have earned their respect as being a person of substance, youre in.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #5  Introverts dont like to go out in public
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Nonsense. Introverts just dont like to go out in public FOR AS LONG. They also like to avoid the complications that are involved in public activities. They take in data and experiences very quickly, and as a result, dont need to be there for long to get it. Theyre ready to go home, recharge, and process it all. In fact, recharging is absolutely crucial for Introverts.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-lwK3K3QnnJ8/UxKcbyNvI-I/AAAAAAAAUTw/yTkPow2CSyY/s1600/introvert6.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                         <img border="0" height="157" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-lwK3K3QnnJ8/UxKcbyNvI-I/AAAAAAAAUTw/yTkPow2CSyY/s1600/introvert6.jpg" width="320"/>
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <br/>
                       <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                        <a href="http://www.jamesdazouloute.net/2014/03/are-you-introvert-like-me-and-how-to.html" target="_blank">
                         <img alt=" How to care for an introvert..." border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-N_4TKLyMYMA/UxKcPMkF9MI/AAAAAAAAUTk/ar096jmVbuo/s1600/introvert3.jpeg"/>
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #6  Introverts always want to be alone
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Introverts are perfectly comfortable with their own thoughts. They think a lot. They daydream. They like to have problems to work on, puzzles to solve. But they can also get incredibly lonely if they dont have anyone to share their discoveries with. They crave an authentic and sincere connection with ONE PERSON at a time.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #7  Introverts are weird.
                       </strong>
                       <br/>
                       Introverts are often individualists. They dont follow the crowd. Theyd prefer to be valued for their novel ways of living. They think for themselves and because of that, they often challenge the norm. They dont make most decisions based on what is popular or trendy.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #8  Introverts are aloof nerds
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Introverts are people who primarily look inward, paying close attention to their thoughts and emotions. Its not that they are incapable of paying attention to what is going on around them, its just that their inner world is much more stimulating and rewarding to them.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #9  Introverts dont know how to relax and have fun
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Introverts typically relax at home or in nature, not in busy public places. Introverts are not thrill seekers and adrenaline junkies. If there is too much talking and noise going on, they shut down. Their brains are too sensitive to the neurotransmitter called Dopamine. Introverts and Extroverts have different dominant neuro-pathways. Just look it up.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong>
                        Myth #10  Introverts can fix themselves and become Extroverts
                       </strong>
                       .
                       <br/>
                       Introverts cannot fix themselves and deserve respect for their natural temperament and contributions to the human race. In fact, one study (Silverman, 1986) showed that the percentage of Introverts increases with IQ.
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       Source:http://www.carlkingdom.com/10-myths-about-introverts
                       <br/>
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <span style="color: red; font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;">
                        <b>
                         <u>
                          Facts About Being An Introvert And The Way You
                         </u>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <span style="color: red; font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;">
                        <b>
                         <u>
                          <br/>
                         </u>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <u>
                        <span style="color: red; font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif; font-size: large;">
                         <b>
                          Live Your
                         </b>
                        </span>
                        <b style="color: red; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: x-large;">
                         Life
                        </b>
                       </u>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <u>
                        <b style="color: red; font-family: Georgia, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: x-large;">
                         <br/>
                        </b>
                       </u>
                      </div>
                      <div style="line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        --You find small talk incredibly cumbersome.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        <strong style="border: 0px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         --You go to parties - but not to meet people.
                        </strong>
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        <strong style="border: 0px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         <strong style="border: 0px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          --You often feel alone in a crowd.
                         </strong>
                        </strong>
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="font-family: Georgia; font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        <strong style="border: 0px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         <strong style="border: 0px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          --
                         </strong>
                        </strong>
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        Networking
                       </strong>
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                        (Small-talk with the end goal of advancing your career)
                       </span>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        makes you feel like a phony.
                       </strong>
                      </div>

                       <h2 style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-family: ProximaNovaSemibold, Helvetica, Arial; font-size: 26px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        This is your inner monologue during after-work drinks.
                       </h2>

                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         --
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         Downtime doesnt feel unproductive to you. (
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         Performers like
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://www.hollyscoop.com/lady-gaga/lady-gaga-admits-she-doesnt-fit-in-to-hollywood-scene.html" sl-processed="1" style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #6aa3b1; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;" target="_hplink">
                         Lady Gaga
                        </a>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         , Christina Aguilera and Emma Watson all
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/08/13/famous-introverts_n_3733400.html" sl-processed="1" style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #6aa3b1; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;" target="_hplink">
                         identify as introverts
                        </a>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         , and an estimated
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/08/05/an-introverts-office-surv_n_3670946.html" sl-processed="1" style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #6aa3b1; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;" target="_hplink">
                         40 percent of CEOs
                        </a>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         have introverted personalities).
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         --You
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         sit in places where you can get away when you're ready to.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         When you get on a Bus, you sit at the end of the bench - not in the middle.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         <br/>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </div>

                       <h2 style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-family: ProximaNovaSemibold, Helvetica, Arial; font-size: 26px; font-weight: normal; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        If anyone ever throws you a fun surprise party, this is your reaction.

                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">

                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        You start to shut down after youve been active for too long.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        --
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        You actively avoid any shows or classes that might involve audience participation.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        --
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        You screen all your calls -- even from friends.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">

                        You have a constantly running inner monologue.
                       </strong>

                        <a href="http://www.jamesdazouloute.net/2014/03/are-you-introvert-like-me-and-how-to.html" target="_blank">
                         <img alt="Agreeing to a lot of nights out in a row isn't fun. AT. ALL." class="bf_dom" height="625" rel:bf_bucket="progload" rel:bf_image_src="http://s3-ec.buzzfed.com/static/enhanced/webdr06/2013/5/31/15/enhanced-buzz-32228-1370027017-11.jpg" src="http://s3-ec.buzzfed.com/static/enhanced/webdr06/2013/5/31/15/enhanced-buzz-32228-1370027017-11.jpg" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;" width="625"/>
                        </a>
                       </div>
                       <div class="sub_buzz_source_via buzz_attribution" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; color: #999999; font-family: ProximaNovaRegular, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; font-style: italic; line-height: 15px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        imgur.com
                       </div>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        --
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        Youve been called an old soul - since your 20s.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        --
                       </strong>
                       <strong style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        You look at the big picture.
                       </strong>
                      </div>
                      <div style="orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         --
                        </span>
                        <span style="border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                         Youre a writer.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         Most introverts --
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                        </span>
                        <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/08/13/famous-introverts_n_3733400.html" sl-processed="1" style="border: 0px; color: #6aa3b1; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;" target="_hplink">
                         like "Harry Potter" author J.K. Rowling
                        </a>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #333333; font-family: Georgia, Century, Times, serif; font-size: 15px; line-height: 21px;">
                         -- say that they feel most creatively charged when they have time to be alone with their thoughts.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </div>
